focus = {
	id = SOV_Down_With_Nep
	icon = GFX_SOV_down_with_nep
	relative_position_id = SOV_Establishing_A_Big_Tent_Party
	x = -1
	y = 2
	cost = 5
	available = { has_country_flag = SOV_decided_to_go_down_with_nep }
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SOV_Premier_Kirov
		focus = SOV_Premier_Tomsky
		focus = SOV_Premier_Rykov
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 100 }
	completion_reward = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_Nikolay_D_Kondratiev_eco_rso }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_Nikolay_D_Kondratiev_eco_rso
				add_idea = RUS_Timofey_V_Sapronov_eco_rso
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_government = radical_socialist 
				NOT = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Sergey Kirov"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_leader_ideology = radsoc_communism_subtype
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_government = radical_socialist 
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Sergey Kirov"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			set_country_leader_ideology = moderate_socialist_subtype
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = rus_nep_14
			add_idea = rus_down_with_nep
		}
		complete_national_focus = RUS_First_Five_Year_Plan
		complete_national_focus = RUS_Form_Gosplan
	}
}

focus = {
	id = SOV_Allow_Small_Traders
	text = RUS_Allow_Small_Traders
	icon = GFX_RUS_Allow_Small_Traders
	cost = 5
	prerequisite = { focus = SOV_Introduce_NEP }
	relative_position_id = SOV_Premier_Bukharin
	x = 1
	y = 2
	available = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = nsp_in_power
			has_idea = RUS_Nikolay_I_Bukharin_hog_syn
		}
	}
	bypass = { has_idea = rus_nep_14 }
	ai_will_do = { factor = 40 }
	completion_reward = {
		country_event = rusdem.314
		if = { #has initial
			limit = { has_idea = rus_nep }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = rus_nep
				add_idea = rus_nep_2
			}
		}
		else_if = { # has smychka
			limit = { has_idea = rus_nep_1 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = rus_nep_1
				add_idea = rus_nep_6
			}
		}
		else_if = { # has cautious industrialization
			limit = { has_idea = rus_nep_4 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = rus_nep_4
				add_idea = rus_nep_8
			}
		}
		else_if = { # has kulaks
			limit = { has_idea = rus_nep_5 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = rus_nep_5
				add_idea = rus_nep_10
			}
		}
		else = { # has kulaks + cautious industrialization
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = rus_nep_12
				add_idea = rus_nep_13
			}
		}
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 217 decision = RUS_Develop_Civilian_Industry_In_State } #Tsaritsyn
	}
}

			limit = { has_idea = rus_unfinished_land_reform }

			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_state_category = four

					has_state_category = two
					has_state_category = one
				}
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_capitalism_in_village_modifier	}
		}
	}
}

	icon = GFX_focus_SOV_breadbasket_of_the_union
	relative_position_id = SOV_Labour_Republic
	x = 3
	y = 3
	cost = 5
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SOV_Cooperative_Agrarain_Economy
	}
	available = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = SOV_Left_SR_Countercoup }
			has_completed_focus = SOV_Elect_The_New_Chairman
		}
		OR = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = plsr_in_power
				OR = {
					has_idea = RUS_Maria_A_Spiridonova_hog_rso
					has_idea = RUS_Yakov_Fishman_hog_tot
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = lpsr_in_power
				has_idea = RUS_Vladimir_K_Volsky_hog_rso
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 20
	}
	available_if_capitulated = yes
	cancel_if_invalid = yes
	continue_if_invalid = no
	
	completion_reward = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = SOV_labour_republic_3
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SOV_labour_republic_3
				add_idea = SOV_labour_republic_4
			}
		}
		else = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = rural_obschina
				add_idea = SOV_rural_independence
			}
		}
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 254 decision = RUS_Mechanize_Agriculture_In_State } #Simbirsk
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 246 decision = RUS_Mechanize_Agriculture_In_State } #Simbirsk
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 258 decision = RUS_Mechanize_Agriculture_In_State } #Simbirsk
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 260 decision = RUS_Mechanize_Agriculture_In_State } #Simbirsk
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 265 decision = RUS_Mechanize_Agriculture_In_State } #Simbirsk
	}
}

			}

				has_idea = SOV_sokolnikov_nep_4
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SOV_sokolnikov_nep_4
				add_idea = SOV_sokolnikov_nep_5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = SOV_sokolnikov_nep_3
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SOV_sokolnikov_nep_3

			}
		}
		else = {

			}

			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_Kaganovich_Economy_Focus_1
					add_idea = SOV_Kaganovich_Economy_Focus_3
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = kaganovich_security_focus }
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_Kaganovich_Security_Focus_1
					add_idea = SOV_Kaganovich_Security_Focus_3
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_Individual_Is_Nothing_tooltip
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = SOV_Kaganovich_Security_Focus_1 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_Kaganovich_Security_Focus_1
					add_idea = SOV_Kaganovich_Security_Focus_3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = SOV_Kaganovich_Security_Focus_2 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_Kaganovich_Security_Focus_2
					add_idea = SOV_Kaganovich_Security_Focus_4
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = SOV_Kaganovich_Economy_Focus_1 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_Kaganovich_Economy_Focus_1
					add_idea = SOV_Kaganovich_Economy_Focus_3
				}
			}
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_Kaganovich_Economy_Focus_2
					add_idea = SOV_Kaganovich_Economy_Focus_4
				}
			}
		}
	}

shared_focus = {
	id = RUS_Support_Anticolonial_Uprisings
	icon = GFX_UKR_Colonial_Problem
	relative_position_id = SOV_Enemy_In_The_West
	x = 4
	y = 4
	cost = 2
	available = { is_subject = no }
	prerequisite = { focus = SOV_Assert_Our_Influence_Far_East }
	prerequisite = { focus = SOV_India_Policy }
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 25
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_war = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_stability < 0.3
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = INC }
			INC = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = KR_close_allies 
				}
			}
			INC = { give_military_access = ROOT }
		}
		else = {
			GEA = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt
				}
			}
			unlock_decision_tooltip = RUS_Liberate_Indochina
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = INS }
			INS = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = KR_close_allies 
				}
			}
			INS = { give_military_access = ROOT }
		}
		else = {
			DEI = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt
				}
			}
			unlock_decision_tooltip = RUS_Liberate_Insulindia
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = MAF }
			MAF = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt
				}
			}
			unlock_decision_tooltip = RUS_Liberate_Afrika
		}
	}
}
